name:N‚Äçe‚Äçi‚Äçl‚Äç ‚ÄçT‚Äçh‚Äço‚Äçm‚Äça‚Äçs
info:Rock Royalty Gold Room
info:Stayed in December 2023
info:1 Review
info:Couples
rating:4.7
posted:Posted December 29, 2023
msg:The Hotel staff was amiable and accommodating.  Although very little English was spoken, the staff tried to speak Cantonese to my wife. We were upgraded to a suite which was clean and very big.  Our package included a daily buffet breakfast and VIP lounge access for a light meal in the evening.  We were given choices out of 4 sets.  The set meal in the lounge was average but it was very cosy and quiet with all kinds of drinks available.

The best part of the hotel was the bathtub with a view!  

The buffet breakfast was OK.  Tea and coffee were very average.  You get better quality from your room.  There are a variety of international cable TV channels.  To my disappointment, the very latest international movie collections come with a daily flat rate.   The size of the TV is a bit small compared to the size of the suite.  The sound bar was fantastic though.

We were very happy that we did not smell cigarette smoke in the hotel except near the smoking venue.  

The hotel is very easy to get to by the underground train.  You can have weatherproof access to the gigantic mall across the road via the train station.  Hard Rock Hotel is positioned to take advantage of the local facilities for a family holiday.  It is very popular with families from HK.
----------------------------------------

msg:Customer Service 
This hotel was booked for my friend‚Äôs 31st birthday. A representative, Ms. Moon, gave us her we chat so my friends and I could communicate with her. Upon arrival, we were checked in my Ms. Bella. She spoke English well and this made it easy to communicate with her. The gentleman at the front door during our stay was also very helpful. A get Customer Service Team.

Amenities 
The room was very spacious. The. bathroom is good size. It has a huge mirror, a shower plus a massive bath tub. The room was clean. It was quite welcoming. The only minor thing is that there was only one bath robe but upon request we received more. There was a also a huge standing mirror at the entrance of the room. Wine glasses were also in the room. 

There is also a pool, that is clean and at the time empty when we went there .

Concierge 
The Concierge not only collected but delivered the package I had shipped to the hotel to my room. That was appreciated. So is you need to ship something you can access that service as well. 

Food 
The buffet style breakfast was awesome as well. There was a wide variety of Western food. There was so many options to choose from. The employees in the buffet restaurant was also very helpful. 

Dinner at Hard Rock Restaurant 
We had dinner at Hard Rock Restaurant downstairs the hotel. The food was really good and the prices were also affordable. There was a live show and the singer sang some a few songs for my friend‚Äôs birthday. The restaurant staff was extremely warm and helpful.

It was a great weekend and we all said we want to go back to Hard Rock Hotel soon.

name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:The GG BOND Party Kids Themed
info:Stayed in May 2024

info:1 Review

posted:Posted May 25, 2024
msg:Hard Rock Hotel Shenzhen was born for rock and roll. Guitar and rock elements are everywhere in the hotel. There is a huge guitar on the outer wall of the hotel, which represents HARD ROCK with a long history. The ceiling of the lobby on the first floor of the hotel is a shining golden dragon flying, which is particularly special. The special thing is that it is artistically combined with pieces of metal on a drum set, which will definitely amaze everyone who sees it. In the lobby on the first floor, you can also see many items used by European and American stars, including costumes of the famous Elvis Presley.
              When you go up to the second floor of the hotel, you can see an entire wall made of real electric guitars. It is estimated that only HARD ROCK has such a large amount of effort to realize such a shocking art decoration.
               The hotel staff checked me in enthusiastically, quickly and accurately. Thank you to these young friends, it's great! I want more MARK, he enthusiastically provided me with effective service. 
                The hotel's buffet restaurant is on the 5th floor, and it's also where I have breakfast.
               The hotel room was great! There is a big bathtub, the deluxe room also has a sofa, and the TV in the room can be adjusted to any angle. It really feels like ROCK. Other hotels really don't have such a function.
                The gym is on the 6th floor of the hotel, and there is a children's playground on the same floor. I went to swim in the swimming pool on the 26th floor. There were so many cute children playing in the water with their families. It was so fun!
                It is very convenient to go from the hotel to the MALL opposite. You can get there through the subway tunnel in front of the hotel. It is also very close to the ski resort in the sports commune. You can just walk to Exit A of the subway station. There is a tunnel right in front of the hotel. Shenzhen's latest and most popular greenway, "Niuhu Water Greenway", is right in front of the hotel. I didn't expect it to be so convenient. MARK told me this information. Otherwise, I would have spent most of the day on this. groping.
               In short, you should come to Shenzhen HARD ROCK, it will definitely make your trip worthwhile.
